[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview of Root Cause  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The out-of-memory condition arises from two issues:  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m In `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE`, there is no upper bound on the number of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacters [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`len`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m used to create a Java `String`, allowing a malicious `len` to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mballoon into a huge char buffer.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m In `MAPIAttribute.create`, the code does an unbounded allocation of `new [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mmplen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` based on parsed input [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mplen`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, then feeds it into [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`getFromUnicodeLE`, bypassing any “safe” allocation logic.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Behavior  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing offset- and negative-length checks in `getFromUnicodeLE` remain [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintact.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We continue to decode byte arrays into Java `String`s using UTF-16LE.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to fuzz harness, test code, or any external [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependencies—only production source files are patched.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Strengthen `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE` with a maximum-size check  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add an `import org.apache.poi.util.IOUtils;` at the top of `StringUtil.java`. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Immediately after validating `offset` and `len` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., before calling the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`String` constructor[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, insert a check that the requested bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m do not [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceed `IOUtils.MAX_RECORD_LENGTH`. For example:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     long byteLen = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlong[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mlen * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyteLen > IOUtils.MAX_RECORD_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mIllegalArgumentException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"UnicodeLE string length exceeds safe [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mmaximum: "[0m[39m + len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This enforces a hard cap on the size of any `String` created via this method, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreventing out-of-memory crashes.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Use safe allocation in `MAPIAttribute.create`  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the unbounded `new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mmplen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` with:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m mpdata = [0m[1;35mIOUtils.safelyAllocate[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmplen, IOUtils.MAX_RECORD_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This mirrors the pattern already used in `TNEFAttribute`, ensuring `mplen` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mitself is bounded by the same global `MAX_RECORD_LENGTH`.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserve existing read/failure logic:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mIOUtils.readFully[0m[1;39m([0m[39minp, mpdata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Not enough data to read "[0m[39m + mplen + [0m[32m" bytes for [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mattribute name"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     name = [0m[1;35mStringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpdata, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmplen/[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and Benefits  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Consistent Safety Model**: By reusing `IOUtils.safelyAllocate` and the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mglobal `MAX_RECORD_LENGTH` constant, we centralize memory-size limits across HMEF, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatching the existing safe-allocation strategy in `TNEFAttribute`.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Early Failure vs. OOM**: Both the upstream byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m allocation and the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdownstream `String` constructor now throw predictable exceptions [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`IllegalArgumentException` or `IOException`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when size limits are exceeded, rather[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthan blowing the heap.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Minimal Impact**: Valid, well-formed documents with reasonable attribute [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnames remain unaffected. Edge-case strings larger than the configured [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MAX_RECORD_LENGTH` simply trigger a controlled exception instead of a crash.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side-Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Legitimate Large Strings**: If real-world HMEF streams legitimately carry [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnames or text near or above the default threshold, users may now see exceptions. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMitigation: allow configuration of `MAX_RECORD_LENGTH` via the standard POI [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontrols [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `org.apache.poi.POIXMLSettings.setMaxRecordLength`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before parsing,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mso users can raise the cap if truly needed.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Odd-Length Data**: As before, odd `mplen` values still lead to [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minteger‐division in `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmplen/[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`. If desired, an additional check for evenness [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`mplen % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m could be added, but this is orthogonal to the memory exhaustion [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfix.  [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. No Harness or Test Changes  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`POIHMEFFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and all test suites remain untouched. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix is purely in the core parsing logic, preserving all existing APIs, behavior[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor valid inputs, and coverage by existing tests.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external libraries or dependencies are modified.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis strategy fully addresses the low-severity OOM alert by bounding both [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte‐array allocation and character conversion, aligning with proven patterns [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39melsewhere in the codebase, without altering test or harness logic.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue involves a Java out-of-memory crash reported by Jazzer when [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing Apache POI’s HMEF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTNEF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m parsing. The exception is a [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueLow` caused by [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space`, originating in [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE` during HMEF message processing. [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA patch attempt was made to introduce bounds checks on allocations:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE`, import `IOUtils`, compute the requested byte [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength as a `long`, and throw an `IllegalArgumentException` if it exceeds [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOUtils.MAX_RECORD_LENGTH`.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `MAPIAttribute.create`, replace `new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mmplen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` with [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mIOUtils.safelyAllocate[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmplen, IOUtils.MAX_RECORD_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to guard against [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moversized allocations.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the patch, the build fails in the `poi` module:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mStringUtil.java: error: cannot find symbol[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyteLen > IOUtils.MAX_RECORD_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                         ^[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  symbol:   variable MAX_RECORD_LENGTH[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  location: class org.apache.poi.util.IOUtils[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdditionally, an unchecked-cast warning appears in `GenericRecordUtil`, but the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfatal error is the missing `MAX_RECORD_LENGTH` symbol.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Initial Issue[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A fuzzer invocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`POIHMEFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggered a Java [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-space exhaustion in the Unicode-LE string decoding routine.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Stack trace highlights:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `StringUtil.<init>[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString.jav[0m[1;92ma:657[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `[0m[1;35mStringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE[0m[1;39m([0m[39mStringUtil.jav[0m[1;92ma:94[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • HMEF message parsing in `TNEFMAPIAttribute`, `TNEFAttribute`, and [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`HMEFMessage`.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Jazzer classifies the crash as a low-severity security issue but flags it as a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreproducible OOM with `-Xmx921m`.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Observations from the Initial Log[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The failure occurs in core POI code, not in the fuzzer harness itself.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Large or corrupted input can lead to a massive `len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m` allocation without upper[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbound checks.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No existing guard in `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE` against unreasonably large [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlengths.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `MAPIAttribute`, raw `new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mmplen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` is used without size validation.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Attempt Details[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **StringUtil.java**  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Added `import org.apache.poi.util.IOUtils;`  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Before allocating the new `String`, compute `long byteLen = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlong[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;`  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `byteLen > IOUtils.MAX_RECORD_LENGTH`, throw `IllegalArgumentException`.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **MAPIAttribute.java**  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Changed `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m mpdata = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mmplen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - To `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m mpdata = [0m[1;35mIOUtils.safelyAllocate[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmplen, IOUtils.MAX_RECORD_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese changes aim to enforce a maximum on in-memory buffers to prevent OOM.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Result and Build Output[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The build output for the `poi` module shows:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Missing symbol `IOUtils.MAX_RECORD_LENGTH` in `StringUtil.java`  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Several unrelated deprecation and unchecked-cast warnings, notably in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`GenericRecordUtil.java`.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The compilation failure is:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- As a result, the `:poi:compileJava` task fails and the Docker‐based fuzzing build[0m [2m                [0m
